{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:39","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:39","title":"Teenage Engineering OB–4 Dials up the Nostalgia of the Mixtape","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=430401","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/teenage-engineering-ob-4-dials-up-the-nostalgia-of-the-mixtape/teenageengineering_radio-7/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-7-810x594.jpg\" alt=\"Teenage Engineering OB–4 Dials up the Nostalgia of the Mixtape\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>While the contemporary silhouettes of wireless audio devices steer ever further into the realm of the amorphous and ambiguous [see: new <a href=\"https://store.google.com/product/nest_audio\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Google Nest</a>], industrial designers operating in more niche realms of home audio are still tapping into the collective memory of pre-digital devices like turntables, cassette players and portable audio systems. The imprint those analog devices have left with their tactile dials and buttons have reemerged in the form of the new <a href=\"https://teenage.engineering/products/ob-4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Teenage Engineering OB-4</a>, a minimalist boombox that recaptures the joy of the mixtape.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430436\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430436\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430436\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-1-810x547.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"547\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-1-810x547.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-1-800x541.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-1-768x519.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/rVYl9UKhvbk\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"><span data-mce-type=\"bookmark\" style=\"display: inline-block; width: 0px; overflow: hidden; line-height: 0;\" class=\"mce_SELRES_start\">﻿</span></iframe></p>\n<p>With its handled design, prominent dial controls and the two 4&#8243; bass drivers and a pair of neodymium tweeters, it&#8217;s obvious Swedish electronics boutique brand Teenage Engineering has an affinity for rewinding back to the past – an idea taken to the highest degree with the inclusion of a manual &#8220;tape&#8221; dial intended to record then &#8220;rewind, time-stretch and loop at the flick of your fingertips&#8221;. It&#8217;s a nifty nod to the days of the &#8220;press play+record&#8221; mixtape, and a feature which Teenage Engineering hints will offer a multitude of greater music creation options using &#8220;disk mode&#8221;:</p>\n<blockquote><p>If you skip the traditional inputs like line in, bluetooth and FM radio, you end up in disk mode. This is where  we will continuously develop new experimental features for the OB–4. it&#8217;s our public research space, where we allow ourselves to explore and prototype everything that this media-instrument, as we call it, can become. for now, there are three functions on the disk; ambient, karma and metronome.</p></blockquote>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430435\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430435\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430435\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-0-810x490.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"490\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-0-810x490.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-0-800x484.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-0-768x464.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-0.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430407\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430407\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430407\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-6-810x627.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"627\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-6-810x627.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-6-800x619.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-6-768x595.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-6.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The wireless speaker system is plenty loud, rated for 38 watts per channel and capable of producing approximately 100 decibels thanks to a Class D amplifier within. You&#8217;ll get back up to 72 hours of playback, or 8 hours at full blast. There&#8217;s no cassette player, but a line input, Bluetooth and built-in FM radio should satisfy a listener&#8217;s desire for future nostalgia in the figurative and literal sense.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430404\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430404\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430404\" 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430405\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430405\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430405\" https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-4-768x860.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/TeenageEngineering_Radio-4.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>An optional $400 OB–4 leather bag and strap made by London brand, Bill Amberg Studio, is joined by a $649 gloss red edition if the $599 matte black finish of the standard OB-4 is too sedate.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430406\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430406\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430406\" 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Unfortunately this first batch of OB-4s has already sold out in both editions. But Teenage Engineering is promising a second batch expected to arrive around a month from now, with reservations being taken <a href=\"https://teenage.engineering/store/ob-4/?color=black\" 03:11:39","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:39","title":"JDWA Transforms an Empty Attic Into a Contemporary Workspace for Upfield","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=430927","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/jdwa-transforms-an-empty-attic-into-a-contemporary-workspace-for-upfield/jdwa-the-attic-sustainable-upfield-office-1/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/JDWA-The-Attic-Sustainable-Upfield-Office-1-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"JDWA Transforms an Empty Attic Into a Contemporary Workspace for Upfield\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>When the Unilever brand split from their margarine and spread department, they had it continue as its own independent company named Upfield. The formation of the new company would unite all of their Rotterdam departments, including the offices, research &#38; development, logistics and production, under one roof on the unused upper floors of a building complex. The Dutch office of <a href=\"https://jdwa.nl/featured-projects/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">JDWA</a> (Johan de Wachter Architecten) were hired to make it happen and they transformed those top stories into a sustainable, contemporary office called <a href=\"https://jdwa.nl/upfield-office-the-attic/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">The Attic</a>.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430929\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430929\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430929\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/JDWA-The-Attic-Sustainable-Upfield-Office-2-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/JDWA-The-Attic-Sustainable-Upfield-Office-2-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/JDWA-The-Attic-Sustainable-Upfield-Office-2-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/JDWA-The-Attic-Sustainable-Upfield-Office-2-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/JDWA-The-Attic-Sustainable-Upfield-Office-2-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/JDWA-The-Attic-Sustainable-Upfield-Office-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The Attic is located in the oldest factory building at the office complex, which meant loads of historical details throughout. To create the modern office inside of an older building, the architects intervened in various ways, like removing unnecessary walls, building out meeting rooms for group work sessions, telephone calls and product displays. Each of the spaces are separated into their own zones with their own schemes, all filled with light and views looking out to the river Maas.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430930\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430930\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430930\" 2020","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=431024","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/5-highlights-you-should-know-about-from-detroit-month-of-design-2020/detroit-month-of-design-tribute-in-light-featured/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/detroit-month-of-design-tribute-in-light-featured-810x530.jpg\" alt=\"5 Highlights You Should Know About From Detroit Month of Design 2020\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Detroit recently concluded its annual <a href=\"https://designcore.org/month-of-design/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">Detroit Month of Design</a> extravaganza led by Design Core Detroit. This year was extra special as it marked their 10th edition of the design festival and although many events were virtual this year, it only allowed even more participants across the country to discover the creativity and spirit of Detroit. Today we&#8217;re recapping five events that we especially loved in this year&#8217;s program:</p>\n<p><iframe src=\"https://player.vimeo.com/video/462645435\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p>\n<p><strong>1. Design in the City</strong><br />\nThis platform gives emerging fashion + accessory designers the opportunity to work with leaders from the fashion industry to further develop their business. This includes receiving invaluable knowledge in marketing support, technical assistance, mentorship, distribution opportunities and more. At the same time, the program helps designers showcase their work and build brand awareness.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_431025\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431025\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431025\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"wp-image-431025 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/detroit-month-of-design-tribute-in-light-1-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/detroit-month-of-design-tribute-in-light-1-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/detroit-month-of-design-tribute-in-light-1-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/detroit-month-of-design-tribute-in-light-1-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/detroit-month-of-design-tribute-in-light-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Paul Taylor Firms</p></div>\n<p><strong>2. Detroit Tribute in Light</strong><br />\nThe Grand Army of the Republic Building (Detroit’s iconic castle across from Beacon Park) was lit aglow with a moving video light show put on by the Downtown Detroit Partnership, Mindfield, and TLS productions. The show illuminated Detroit’s suffering and strength in the face of two pandemics, Covid-19 and racial injustice.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_431026\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431026\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431026\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"wp-image-431026 size-large\" https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/detroit-month-of-design-tribute-in-light-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Paul Taylor Noah Elliot Morrison</p></div>\n<p><strong>3. Local Color: Natural Dyes of Detroit</strong><br />\nA zen-like public installation that can be safely viewed at The Delinquindre Cut (on 1905 Alfred St), Local Color showcased the beautiful and natural hues of plants grown and foraged in Detroit through a series of tapestries woven by weaver + artist <a href=\"https://www.salttextilestudios.com/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">Kayla Powers of Salt Textile Studios</a>.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_431030\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a <em>Intelligent(1)Degenerate(2)</em>, Heron Robinson with<em> Astro//Black</em>, Mariana Sanchez with <em>Lovour,</em> and Tori Abrahams with <em>Metamorphosis.</em></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_431033\" 03:11:39","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:39","title":"DMTV Milkshake: Katie Treggiden Is Making Sense of Waste","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=430802","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/dmtv-milkshake-katie-treggiden-is-making-sense-of-waste/dmtv_milkshake_featured_image_and_slider-katie-treggiden/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/DMTV_Milkshake_Featured_Image_and_Slider-Katie-Treggiden-810x536.jpg\" alt=\"DMTV Milkshake: Katie Treggiden Is Making Sense of Waste\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>This week’s Milkshake guest is our very own <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/author/katie/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Editor at Large</a>, author and speaker Katie Treggiden, who recently released her latest book <a href=\"http://hyperurl.co/h991kp\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><em>Wasted: When Trash Becomes Treasure</em></a>, which examines waste in design.</p>\n<p>“My question is always, &#8216;now what?&#8217;” says author and speaker Katie Treggiden, whose book <a href=\"http://hyperurl.co/h991kp\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><em>Wasted: When Trash Becomes Treasure</em></a> arrives in bookstores this month. She’s referring specifically to the problem of furniture items marketed as heirloom treasures, the sort of the piece designed to be handed from one generation to the next. “At some point, that object is going to become obsolete,” Treggiden says. “So we&#8217;ve really got to think about the end of life of the objects we&#8217;re designing, even if they&#8217;re designed to last for a really long time.”</p>\n<p><iframe src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/c891ciUMtMA\" width=\"810\" height=\"455\" frameborder=\"0\" allowfullscreen=\"allowfullscreen\"></iframe></p>\n<p>That idea – of impermanence and its costs – filters through much of the work showcased in <em>Wasted, </em>like the U.K. designer Aimee Bollu’s vessels, crafted to incorporate a specific piece of waste, like a single stalk of dried purple broccoli. In her video, Katie also shares how she confronts conspicuous waste on the personal level (<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=rhcKuMjvcCk\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><em>Mad Men</em> viewers will recognize a certain picnic-centric motif</a>) – and whether the job of reducing waste will best fall to government, corporations or the consumer, who’s been told to reduce, reuse and recycle since birth. “While I think that it&#8217;s incredibly important for us to claim our personal agency and make the difference that we can to our personal waste footprints, I think we&#8217;ve also got to start pushing back up the chain,” she says. “There are people who’ll take everything out of the packing at the till at the supermarket and leave it all there for the cashier to deal with – and while I think that&#8217;s unfair to the cashier, it does send the message back to the supermarket: We don&#8217;t want all that plastic wrapped around our fruit.” <a href=\"http://hyperurl.co/h991kp\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Buy Katie’s book here</a> and read her Design Milk column on this same topic: <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/column/circular-by-design/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Circular By Design</a>.</p>\n<p>View Katie’s DMTV Milkshake episode above, then check out the rest of the series <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLg78zLY1oQztyRgHfo5rKVp1qWAQn8r3k\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">here</a>.</p>\n<p><em>Diana Ostrom, who has written for Wallpaper, Interior Design, ID, The Wall Street Journal, and other outlets, is also the author of </em><a href=\"http://farawayplaces.co/newsletter\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><em>Faraway Places</em></a><em>, a newsletter about travel.</em></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/tag/DMTV-Milkshake/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><em>Milkshake</em></a><em>, DMTV (Design Milk TV)’s first regular series, shakes up the traditional interview format by asking designers, creatives, educators and industry professionals to select interview questions at random from their favorite bowl or vessel. During their candid discussions, you’ll not only gain a peek into their personal homeware collections, but also valuable insights into their work, life and passions.</em></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/friday-five-with-jason-wu/f5-jason-wu-0-cropped-headshot/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-0-cropped-headshot-810x564.jpg\" alt=\"Friday Five With Jason Wu\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div id=\"attachment_431126\" 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Laurence Ellis</p></div>\n<p><em><a href=\"https://www.jasonwustudio.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Jason Wu&#8217;s</a> interest in fashion began at an early age, when he would use dolls as mannequins for the miniature garments he would sew. It&#8217;s taken the designer only ten years to create his internationally recognized brand of clothing. Merging classic American sportswear elements and couture, his collection is sold globally. Since debuting his Ready-to-Wear collection in 2007, Wu has been dedicated to making clothing that are beautifully crafted from the inside out. With a focus on quality and traditional craftsmanship, much of his collection is manufactured in New York using custom developed fabrics from the finest mills in France and Italy. Today Wu dresses some of the most influential women in the world, including First Lady Michelle Obama, Reese Witherspoon, Julianne Moore, Diane Kruger, Liu Wen and Christy Turlington, among others. In addition to fashion, Wu has been collaborating with luxury bath and kitchen fixtures brand Brizo® for a decade, starting with the Matte Black Jason Wu for Brizo<img src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/12.0.0-1/72x72/2122.png\" alt=\"™\" class=\"wp-smiley\" style=\"height: 1em; max-height: 1em;\" /> Bath Collection. For Fall 2020, their partnership continues with the launch of the streamlined <a href=\"https://www.brizo.com/kitchen/collection/jason-wu-for-brizo\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Jason Wu for Brizo<img src=\"https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/12.0.0-1/72x72/2122.png\" alt=\"™\" class=\"wp-smiley\" style=\"height: 1em; max-height: 1em;\" /> Kitchen Collection</a> in a signature Matte White finish. Today Jason Wu joins us for <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/column/friday-five/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">Friday Five</a>!</em></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_431127\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431127\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431127\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431127\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-1-Rice-810x1080.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1080\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-1-Rice-810x1080.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-1-Rice-800x1067.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-1-Rice-768x1024.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-1-Rice-1152x1536.jpg 1152w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-1-Rice.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Jason Wu</p></div>\n<p>1. Rice<br />\nI grew up eating rice every day and it is definitely a must on the menu for me weekly (if not daily!). I also love to cook and have recently come up with so many ways to experiment and create dishes with rice, from the traditional Chinese Zongzi, Korean stirred fried rice cake or just a simple “everything in the fridge” fried rice that my mother used to make for us.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_431128\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431128\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431128\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431128\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-2-111-Skin-Celestial-Black-Diamond-Cream-810x765.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"765\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-2-111-Skin-Celestial-Black-Diamond-Cream-810x765.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-2-111-Skin-Celestial-Black-Diamond-Cream-800x756.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-2-111-Skin-Celestial-Black-Diamond-Cream-768x725.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-2-111-Skin-Celestial-Black-Diamond-Cream.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Courtesy of 111 Skin</p></div>\n<p>2. 111 Skin Celestial Black Diamond Cream<br />\nI love a spa day at home and nothing is better after a busy day than to spend some time treating myself to an at-home facial. I love all of the products from <a href=\"https://111skin.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">111 Skin</a>, but my favorite is definitely the Celestial Black Diamond Cream—it’s rich, nourishing and so luxurious. I feel much fresher and more relaxed after some soothing skincare time, combined with some obligatory Netflix time.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_431129\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431129\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431129\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431129\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-3-Travel-810x1080.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1080\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-3-Travel-810x1080.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-3-Travel-800x1067.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-3-Travel-768x1024.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-3-Travel-1152x1536.jpg 1152w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-3-Travel.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Jason Wu</p></div>\n<p>3. Travel<br />\nI love to travel and have been fortunate to visit so many different parts of the world throughout my life. While there is still a long list of places I’d like to go, I find that every time I get to experience a new culture I am immediately inspired. Being able to see new things and learn about traditions from other regions of the world has allowed me to become a fuller person. One of my favorite places to go is Tulum because it is just so beautiful and effortless—I usually come home with a full stack of sketches and new ideas. Japan is also amazing and I can’t wait to be back. It&#8217;s a culture full of modern innovation with impeccably preserved traditions, everything I see and touch has a story behind it and is always so beautifully executed.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_431130\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431130\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431130\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-431130\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-4-Architecture-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-4-Architecture-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-4-Architecture-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-4-Architecture-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-4-Architecture.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Photo: Courtesy of Studio Mellone</p></div>\n<p>4. Architecture<br />\nI caught the architecture bug from my mother, who did not have formal architecture training but had the best sense of style. I remember when we moved to Canada, she chose to buy a house built in the 1950’s and filled the entire house with vintage finds that she would get from markets and furniture shows. Back then I begged her for a new house, because all of my friends were living in new developments that all looked the same—I wanted to fit in. Years later, I find myself to be exactly like my mother! I search the world to buy rare, interesting furniture pieces that have a sense of history and a story behind it. I particularly love the mid-century era because it is my favorite era in design—I&#8217;m often inspired by the clothes of the same era in my designs.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431131\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431131\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-431131\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-5-Apple-iPhone-11-810x743.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"743\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-5-Apple-iPhone-11-810x743.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-5-Apple-iPhone-11-800x734.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-5-Apple-iPhone-11-768x704.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/F5-Jason-Wu-5-Apple-iPhone-11.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>5. iPhone<br />\nEveryone who knows me knows that I live and sleep with my iPhone. In fact, I don’t even own a computer! I use my phone as a kind of a digital journal, taking pictures of things that inspire me and also documenting new ideas and thoughts that I have at any time throughout a day—or sometimes in the middle of the night. I’ve also discovered so many great talents to collaborate with through social media. In fact, I am collaborating with an artist from Japan that I connected with through Instagram this coming season. I love the idea of human connection and through Instagram, I have been able to meet some amazing people who I would have otherwise never met.</p>\n<p><strong>Work by Jason Wu for Brizo:</strong></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_431230\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431230\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431230\" That’s what <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/alder-new-york\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Alder New York</a> creates: vegan products that are dermatologist approved, so you can rest assured and pamper at your leisure knowing you’re putting on only the best ingredients. This queer- and woman-owned independent skincare brand was founded in 2016 by Nina Zilka and David J. Krause who wanted to bring their design sensibility and passion for wellness to their top shelf. 03:11:39","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:39","title":"AeroLyze Breath Glucometer Wins the 2020 US James Dyson Award","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=430237","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/aerolyze-breath-glucometer-wins-the-2020-us-james-dyson-award/aerolyze-aerolyze-tile/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-AeroLyze-tile-810x456.jpeg\" alt=\"AeroLyze Breath Glucometer Wins the 2020 US James Dyson Award\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>More than 1 in 3 Americans – totaling about 88 million – are prediabetic. Unfortunately the majority of that group is unaware of their borderline condition, a missed opportunity to steer a considerable amount of that figure from developing type 2 diabetes, heart disease and stroke. Designer <a href=\"https://thipok.ch/about\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Thipok Poom Cholsaipant&#8217;s</a>&#8216;s AeroLyze aims to simplify testing with the introduction of a small user-friendly and app-connected device designed to test glucose levels without requiring the finger-pricking traditionally needed in testing for diabetes.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430261\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430261\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430261\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Necklace-810x652.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"652\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Necklace-810x652.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Necklace-800x644.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Necklace-768x619.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Necklace.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>While post glucose testing devices require taking a small sample of blood through pinprick, the AeroLyze only needs a single breath to measure blood glucose using acetone analysis. The device incorporates machine learning  to aid in the interpretation of the data, notifying users to become both more aware and proactive in avoiding dangerous glucose levels.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430253\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430253\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430253\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Poom-holding-AeroLyze-810x581.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"581\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Poom-holding-AeroLyze-810x581.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Poom-holding-AeroLyze-800x574.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Poom-holding-AeroLyze-768x551.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Poom-holding-AeroLyze.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430251\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430251\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430251\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-AeroLyze-blueprint-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-AeroLyze-blueprint-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-AeroLyze-blueprint-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-AeroLyze-blueprint-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-AeroLyze-blueprint.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Cholsaipant&#8217;s AeroLyze was awarded this year&#8217;s US <a href=\"https://www.dyson.com/newsroom/overview/features/september-2020/james-dyson-award-winners\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">James Dyson Award</a>, a Y-shaped breath glucometer that allows users to obtain daily glucose level readings conveniently and unobtrusively. The AeroLyze is designed to work in coordination with smartphone and connected wearables, presenting users with an easy to navigate GUI and rating scale interface intended to reduce the anxiety often connected with fluctuating blood glucose levels.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430254\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430254\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430254\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Diagram—App-810x578.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"578\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Diagram—App-810x578.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Diagram—App-800x571.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Diagram—App-768x548.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Diagram—App.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>“The current process for measuring blood sugar levels is a long, painful ritual for just a mere glimpse at a three-digit number,&#8221; says Cholsaipant. &#8220;I believe humans are built from experiences not just numbers. This begs the question: How might we design a better glucose monitoring experience? AeroLyze aims to learn a person’s lifestyle, simplify the testing process and deliver results in a non-invasive way that eliminates misinterpretations.&#8221;</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430255\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430255\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430255\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Diagram—Watch-copy-810x576.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"576\" https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Diagram—Watch-copy-768x547.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Aerolyze-Diagram—Watch-copy.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Cholsaipant&#8217;s design progresses to the international stage of the James Dyson Award where it will compete against other similarly innovative solutions; the young engineer designer plans to use the prize money to finalize and patent the AeroLyze prototype, alongside improving the tool’s machine learning to form improved predictive data about user’s habits to provide more accurate advice for the wearer and user.</p>\n<p>With the arrival of the <a href=\"https://www.apple.com/apple-watch-series-6/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Apple Watch Series 6</a> and its newly integrated SPO2 sensor for blood oxygen level readings joining the smartwatch&#8217;s existing ECG sensor introduced with the Series 4 model, it&#8217;s evident wearable health technologies like the AeroLyze represent a new era of wearable technology relying upon machine learning to offer proactive and preventative solutions, with scale and cost as the primary barrier in reaching those 88 million with prediabetic numbers.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430256\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430256\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-Featured-Image-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"GUBI Releases New Pacha Designs by Pierre Paulin\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Iconic designer Pierre Paulin spent years studying comfort in an effort to create the feeling of sitting on clouds. While his <a href=\"https://shop.gubi.com/pages/pacha-collection\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Pacha collection</a> was a few decades ahead of its time in 1975, it&#8217;s being reissued today by <a href=\"https://shop.gubi.com\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">GUBI</a>. Modular by design, the Pacha Lounge Chair, the Pacha Lounge Chair with armrests, a pair of Pacha Sofas with two to five seats and the Pacha Ottoman give you the ability to create configurations or use each piece alone. The sofas are made by connecting modules with an optional armrest between each pair.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430746\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430746\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430746\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-1-810x1213.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1213\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-1-810x1213.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-1-800x1198.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-1-768x1150.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-1.jpg 1000w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>Jacob Gubi, Owner and Creative Director of GUBI, says: “Pierre Paulin created so many iconic designs, it seems wrong that the Pacha Collection has been edited out of his story. GUBI is delighted to reissue this timeless and characterful collection and play a part in building Paulin the legacy he deserves.”</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430747\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430747\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430747\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-2-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-2-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-2-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-2-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-2.jpg 1000w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The contemporary curved forms of the Pacha collection were designed to serve the human body with rounded outlines and proportions for extreme comfort. Paulin brought a modern elegance to the robust forms by tracing the foam and upholstery with inward-inclined stitching lines to enhance its shape. The Pacha collection is ready to bring style and character to any space in a wide range of upholstery fabrics and a base in the original pearl gold and matte black.</p>\n<p>GUBI is working closely with <a href=\"https://paulinpaulinpaulin.com/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Paulin, Paulin, Paulin</a> – a family enterprise created to bring Paulin&#8217;s unrealized <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/furniture\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">furniture</a> designs to production – to help realize his ambition and ensure his legacy.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430748\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430748\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430748\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-3-810x1213.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1213\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-3-810x1213.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/GUBI-Pacha-Pierre-Paulin-3-800x1198.jpg 800w, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430749\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430749\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430749\" studiofour","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=430657","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/the-minimalist-ruxton-rise-residence-by-studiofour/ruxtonriseresidence_studiofour_00004/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/ruxtonriseresidence_studiofour_00004-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"The Minimalist Ruxton Rise Residence by studiofour\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"http://www.studiofour.net.au/ruxton-rise-residence-1/wx9ayrudokzjfgl2rj4jgy9u2aoqpi\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Ruxton Rise Residence</a> is a minimalist home located in Melbourne, Australia, designed by <a href=\"http://www.studiofour.net.au/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">studiofour</a>. The home is based on the client&#8217;s three most important life values: family, health and integrity. The home goes beyond a physical structure, but becomes symbolic of the family&#8217;s beliefs.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430664\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430664\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430664\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/ruxtonriseresidence_studiofour_00006-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/ruxtonriseresidence_studiofour_00006-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/ruxtonriseresidence_studiofour_00006-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/ruxtonriseresidence_studiofour_00006-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/ruxtonriseresidence_studiofour_00006-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/ruxtonriseresidence_studiofour_00006.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The architects&#8217; response was to focus on the experience versus creating a visual statement. As such, their approach was a contemporary take on the  Beaumaris mid-century modern home. By reflecting inward, the internal courtyard garden is treated as an extra room within the house.</p>\n<p>The floor plan reflects the client&#8217;s focus on family by designing a space conducive of community and intimacy. With an emphasis on communal spaces, the interior encourages the fostering of relationships, both within the family and with friends.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430680\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430680\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-430680\" 0/10/09/19-12-50-104_8b397a5c53849ed1.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/WBQ-x395CZE":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn37@2020_1/2020/10/09/19-12-47-560_f10909433aec2b82.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602270699718},{"createdTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:39","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:39","title":"Old + New Danish Design Come Together in the Islets Table Collection","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=430757","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/old-new-danish-design-come-together-in-the-islets-table-collection/islets-dining-table-maria-bruun-for-fredericia-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Islets-Dining-Table-Maria-Bruun-for-Fredericia-Featured-Image-810x538.jpg\" alt=\"Old + New Danish Design Come Together in the Islets Table Collection\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>The <a href=\"https://www.fredericia.com/search.aspx?search=islets\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Islets</a> table collection, designed in collaboration between <a href=\"https://www.fredericia.com/designerdetails/by-designer-maria-bruun.aspx?PID=65\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Maria Bruun</a> and <a href=\"https://www.fredericia.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Fredericia</a>, puts the steadfast beauty of Danish design on full display. Bruun represents the new generation of furniture designers with respect for tradition and heritage, and space to bring it into the future. <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/furnishings\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Furniture</a> company Fredericia was established in 1911, and have manufactured some of the most iconic furniture pieces from Denmark since the 1950s.</p>\n<p>“To me, Fredericia is a cornerstone in Danish design history. The strong connection between the past and the future is very unique and a privilege to be part of. Their uncompromising focus on quality is enormously appealing to me as a furniture designer. Our core values are very much aligned,” said Bruun.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430899\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-430899\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-full wp-image-430899\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Islets-Dining-Table-Maria-Bruun-for-Fredericia-1.jpg\" alt=\"dining table\" width=\"810\" height=\"1155\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Islets-Dining-Table-Maria-Bruun-for-Fredericia-1.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Islets-Dining-Table-Maria-Bruun-for-Fredericia-1-800x1141.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/Islets-Dining-Table-Maria-Bruun-for-Fredericia-1-768x1095.jpg 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The Islets collection consists of three tables crafted from solid oak wood. Based on simple construction, precise design and strong identity with a minimum of details, it&#8217;s the result of Bruun exploring the balance between a light minimal expression and a bold presence.</p>\n<p>”My love for solid wood is clearly expressed in Islets. I firmly believe in sustainability through quality. Creating a piece of furniture that is aesthetically pleasing with well thought details, carried out with the best craftsmanship and high-quality materials. With the oak wood, I wanted a material that acts as a pleasing, soft and caring gesture towards its users.”</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=430900\" rel=\"attachment 49-494_1ab9a1913650451e.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602270699723},{"createdTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:39","updatedTime":"2020-10-10 03:11:39","title":"An Apartment on a Residential Yacht That Transforms From One Bedroom To Two","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=431070","description":"\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/an-apartment-on-a-residential-yacht-that-transforms-from-one-bedroom-to-two/mkca_pied-a-mer-apartment-at-sea-1/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-1-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"An Apartment on a Residential Yacht That Transforms From One Bedroom To Two\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>It might look like a regular residence at first glance, but this <a href=\"http://mkca.com/projects/pied-a-mer/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">600-square-foot apartment</a> is located aboard a residential yacht. Designed by <a href=\"http://mkca.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Michael K. Chen Architecture</a> (MKCA), the Pied-å-Mer serves as a couple&#8217;s holiday retreat for themselves and their grown children as it easily transforms to welcome two to four people. MKCA utilized their own knowledge in designing smaller, multifunctional spaces, while referencing Le Corbusier&#8217;s fascination with mid-century steamship design to create the clever convertible floor plan.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431074\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431074\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-431074\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-2-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-2-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-2-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-2-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>The design incorporates convertible designs, like fold-up beds and a collapsing dining table. The main living area features two ribbed aluminum pod-like structures that help organize the space while housing two bathrooms and storage. The open living room turns into the primary bedroom when a cantilevered bed pulls down. A passageway against the wall leads to the main bathroom and closet, which is easily accessed from the bedroom.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431075\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431075\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-431075\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-3-810x1134.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1134\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-3-810x1134.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-3-800x1120.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-3-768x1075.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-3-1097x1536.jpg 1097w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/MKCA_Pied-a-Mer-Apartment-at-Sea-3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p>A seating area on the opposite side of the apartment transforms to a dining area when it&#8217;s time to eat, and then to a second bedroom when needed. A sliding screen surrounds it to give both beds privacy.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431076\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431076\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=431077\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-431077\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/10/cloudnola-flipping-out-clocks-1-810x558.jpg\" alt=\"These cloudnola Clocks Will Have You Flipping Out\" /></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>If you have an appreciation for all things analog, just love <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/clocks\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">clocks</a> or need one to keep time, the Flipping Out clocks from <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/cloudnola\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">cloudnova</a> are a cool option. Flip clocks have been around for decades but they&#8217;re often hard to find in working order. Cloudnova took the idea and gave them a modern spin by removing the outer shell allowing you to see how the clock operates. From the side, you can watch as each leaf falls and reveals the next number. The clocks are large enough to hang on the wall and see from a distance, yet still compact so they fit on a desk or table. Each clock measures 15 inches wide x 5.5 inches tall x 3.5 inches deep and comes in four color options: <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/cloudnola/products/flipping-out-black\"
